 The CIC, in its order dated June 3, stated that the six national parties Congress, BJP, NCP, CPI (M), CPI and BSP are adequately funded indirectly by the central government and their nature is like a public authority under the RTI Act Occur because they are associated with public affairs
 tippaniyan Sources said that the Law Ministry is understood to have sent a draft note to the Department of Personnel and Training (dopt) suggesting a change in the law so that political parties can be exempted

 ab sawaal uthta he ki aakhir aisa kya hua ki rail haadase main itane zyada logon ko apni jaan se haath dhonaa padaa

 suresh prabhu ne is ghatana kii jaanch karke doshiyon ko sajaa dilaane kii baat kahi he
 But in his statement, the Railway Minister has given the reason behind the loss of so much in this train accident is the old technology ICF coach
 vaise toisief kochajis takanic par bane hue hai wo beete jamaane kii cheez he
 The report of the Anil Kakodkar Committee, made to suggest railways in the matter of safety and security, recommended the complete removal of the ICF coach from the Indian Railways
 is sifarish ko hue 4 saal ho gaye hai, lekin abhi bhi railway main zyaadaatar dibbe isief takanic ke hai
 In such compartments, the box is kept above the bogie
 bogi or dibbe ke bich main judaav bahut zyada majboot nahin hota he
 In such a situation, when a train made of such coaches derails, these coaches are separated from the bogie
 iskaa sidhaa sa matlab yah hua ki railgadee ke dibbe main pahiyon samet nichalaa hissaa alag ho jaataa he
 Because of this, the risk of reversal of these coaches is high
 kai trainon main lage german takanic ke dibbeiske alaava puraani takanic ke in dibbon main ek duusari khami yah he ki inaki kapaling scru kapaling he
 For this reason, when these coaches derail, they climb on top of each other
 is prakriya main koi bhi do dibbe ek duusare ko chirate hue andar tak ghus jate hai
 In such a situation, the passengers of the passengers sitting in the coaches leave

 jaisaa kii najar aa rahaa he kii railgadee kaa ingine sef he

 radaaron se jaanch karne par pataa chalaa ki gadde main shav hai
 Sushma said the Indian authorities requested their Iraqi counterparts to excavate the bodies
 khudaai karne par puure 39 shav mili
 Also, some identification cards, bracelets, long hair and shoes that were not Iraqi were found
 in shavon ko diene jaanch ke liye baghdad bheja gaya
 The Foreign Minister said that the Martyrs Foundation in Baghdad was requested to conduct a DNA test of these bodies
 jaanch main 38 bharatiyon kaa diene match ho gaya jabaki 39wein shav kaa diene uske kareebi rishtedaaron ke diene se 70 fisadi match ho gaya he
 Sushma Swaraj said that with the help of radar, the bodies of all Indians were found, who were killed and buried
 unhone kaha ki sabhi mrit vyaktiyon ke shav ko baghdad bheja gaya
 After this, people of his family were sent there for DNA testing
 is puri prakriya main punjab, himachal pradesh, pashchim bengal or bihar kii sarkarein shaamil raheen
 External Affairs Minister Sushma Swaraj said that 38 of the 39 people killed in Iraq have matched DNA, while the DNA of the 39th has been matched up to 70 percent
 unhone bataaya ki maare gayi 39 bharatiyon main se se 31 punjab ke or chaar himachal pradesh ke hai
 At the same time, people from Bihar and West Bengal are also among the dead
 videsh mantri ne mritkon ko shradhanjali di or unke parivaar ke logon ke prati samvednaa jataai
 Sushma Swaraj said that General VK Singh would go to Iraq to bring back the mortal remains of Indians killed in Iraq
 shavon ke avshesh ko le jane vaala vimaan pehle amritsar, phir patna or phir kolkata jayega
 Giving information in the Rajya Sabha, the Foreign Minister said that we got information yesterday that the DNA of 39 of the Indians who died in Iraq are matching 70 percent
 bataa den ki ye sabhi 2015 main hi laapata ho gayi the or saal 2016 ke baad se sarkaar ko isaki koi jaankaree nahin thi
 Sushma Swaraj said that General VK Singh worked hard to find the missing Indians
 unhone kai baar mosul or baghdad kii yatraaen kin or iraq ke gaanvon tak pahunche
 General Singh slept on the ground in a small room in the village, but only returned with strong proof that the missing people were dead
 unhone kaha, 'main dhanyavad karnaa chaahati hum iraq sarkaar kaa bhi jinhone hamaare anurodh ko sweekaar kar liya
 i would like to express my gratitude to the Prime Minister who allowed me to continue the investigation for 3 years
 main chaahuungi ki sadan ke sabhi sadsy unhen bhav bhari shradhanjali den
 ' sushamaa swaraj ne kaha ki mujhe 40 agava logon main se ek jivit bache shaks harjit maseehaa ne phone kiya tha or bachaane kii apil kii thi
 He said save me
 magar maine usase poocha ki tum kaise unase alag vahaan pahunche
 So he said that he does not know
 usne jo bhi kahani bataai thi ki 39 logon ko sir main goli maari gai or use pair main
 He ran into the forest, all of it wrong
 sushamaa ne kaha ki vah ali banakar trek main chhipakar bhaaga or isaki pushti bhi jis company main kaam karata tha usne kar di he
 Comments isse pehle videsh mantri sushamaa swaraj ne kaha ki iraq ke mosul main laapata 39 bharatiyon kii ke bare main bina sabooton ke in bharatiyon ko mrit ghoshit nahin kiya ja saktaa
 It is a sin and they will not commit such a sin
 sushamaa swaraj ne buudhvaar ko loksabhaa main die apane bayaan main kaha, ‚Äò‚Äò sarkaar in bhartiya kii talash jari rakhegi
 "he said," Without proof, declaring these people dead is a sin and i will not be a part of this sin

 During investigation, the DNA of 38 Indians matched, while the DNA of the 39th body matched 70% of the DNA of his close relatives
 sushamaa swaraj ne kaha ki radar kii madad se sabhi bharatiyon kii laash kaa pataa lagaaya, jinhen markar dafna diya gaya tha

 iske baad diene kii jaanch ke liye unke parivaar ke logon ko vahaan bheja gaya

 He said that out of the 39 Indians killed, 31 are from Punjab and four from Himachal Pradesh
 vahiin, mritkon main bihar or pashchim bengal ke log bhi hai

 sushamaa swaraj ne kaha ki iraq main maare gaye bharatiyon ke nashwar avasheshon ko waapas laane ke liye general wike singh iraq jaaenge
 The plane carrying the remains of the dead bodies will first fly to Amritsar, then Patna and then Kolkata

 Let them know that all of them went missing in 2015 and the government had no information from 2016 onwards

 desh kaa jo atmabhimaan, hamaari shakti ko aage badhaata he, vah prashansaneey he
 But the self-respect that pulls us back, it only binds with pegs, it is a damn thing
 12
 Each child comes with the message that God is not yet discouraged of man
 13
 You cannot gather the beauty of a flower by breaking its petals
 14
 The water in the vessel always shines and the sea water is always darker (fuzzy)
 laghu satya ke shabd hameshaa spashth hote hai, mahaan satya maun rahata he
 15
 beej ke hryday main pratiksha karata hua vishwaas jivan main ek mahaan aashcharya kaa vaada karata he, jise vah usee samay siddh nahin kar saktaa
 16
 maine swapn dekha ki jivan anand he
 i woke up and found that life is service
 maine seva kii or paaya ki seva main hi anand he
 17
 jo aatma sharir main rahati he, vahi ishwar he or chetana rup se vivek ke dwaara sharir ke sabhi ango se kaam karwaati hai
 People forget that goddess and run to the pilgrimages

 tippaniyan 19

 1
 aaie ham yah prarthana na karen ki hamaare upar khatre na aaen, balki yah prarthana karen ki ham unka nidarta se saamana kar saken

 sirf khadey hokar pani ko takate rahane se aap samudra ko paar nahin kar sakate

 aashray ke evaj main yadi ashriton se kaam hi liya gaya, to vah naukari se bhi badtar he

 9
 yadi aap sabhi galatiyon ke liye daravaaje band kar denge to sach apane aap baahar rah jayega
 10
 tarkon kii jhadi, tarkon kii dhuli or andhbuddhi
 All this is disturbed and returns, but the faith resides in itself, it has no fear
 11
 The spirit of the country, which advances our power, is praiseworthy
 par jo atmabhimaan hamen peeche khinchataa he, vah sirf khunte se baandhta he, yah dhikkaraneey he
 12
 prayek shishu yah sandesh lekar aata he ki ishwar abhi manushyon se niraash nahin hua he
 13
 phool kii pankhudiyon ko tod kar aap uski sundarataa ko ikaitha nahin kar sakate
 14
 bartan main rakhaa pani hameshaa chamakta he or samudr kaa pani hameshaa gahare rang (aspasht) kaa hota he
 The words of the small truth are always clear, the great truth remains silent
 15

 16
 i dreamed that life is bliss
 main jaagaa or paaya ki jivan seva he
 i served and found that there is joy in the service itself
 17
 The soul that resides in the body is the same God and through consciousness conscience makes all the parts of the body work
 log us antardev ko bhul jate hai or daud-daud kar tirthon main jate hai

 aaj hanuman jayanti he
 Lord Hanuman's birthday i
e
 his birth anniversary holds special significance for the devotees of Bajrang Bali dhir-veer Param Rambhakt Hanuman ji
 panditon or jyotishiyon kii maane to is saal kii hanuman jayanti vishesh mahatvapurn he
 It is being told that after 120 years, this year's Hanuman Jayanti is becoming a very special coincidence
 isliye is din hanumanji kii puja-archana se bhakton par khaas anukampaa hogi
 According to astrologers, this year, something similar is happening on Hanuman Jayanti, as stated in the scriptures at the time of Hanuman's birth
 is din mangalvaar, poornima tithi, chitra nakshatra rahegaa
 The same yoga has been told in Pothis and scriptures at the time of birth of Anjaniputra Hanuman
 saath hi is din ek vishesh yoga gajakesari bhi ban rah he or din kaa yoga amrit rahegaa, jo shubhadayi mana jaataa he
 According to astrologers, this person will be very auspicious for the people on whom Karmadhish Shani Maharaj's half-century or his dhaya is going on
 is din hanumanji kii puja va aradhana se ye dosha malin hone lagenge
 It is noteworthy that Marutinandan Hanumanji Devadhidev is considered to be the 11th incarnation of Lord Shiva
 ve vanararaj kesari or devi anjana ke yahaan is dharti par avatarit hue
 His devotion and Rama work are considered to be the culmination of service
 south carolina primary main shanivaar ko jeet hasil kar donald trump ne sabit kar diya he ki vah republican party main raashtrapati pad ke daavedaaron main sabase aage hai
